<h1 _ngcontent-xri-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="mapCommon（地图属性模型）"> mapCommon（地图属性模型） </h1>

<div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供map组件相关属性设置接口。</p>    <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="section164051883419" <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> class="cellrowborder" width="29.75%">          <p>地图旋转角度。</p>          <p>以正北方向为0度、顺时针方向为正的角度，默认值为0，取值范围：[0, 360)。超出取值范围的值会换算成取值范围内的值，比如361会被换算成1，-1换算为359。</p></td>        </tr> <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section12537418218">ImageOverlayParams</a>、<a <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.6.1.1" width="30%">          <p>名称</p></th>         <th align="left" <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.97%">          <p>是否可见，默认值为true，异常值按默认值处理。</p>          <ul>           <li>true：可见</li>           <li>false：不可见</li>          </ul></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>zIndex</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.45%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.58%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.97%">          <p>覆盖物的叠加顺序，具有较大z指数的覆盖物会绘制在具有较小z指数的覆盖物上，具有相同z指数的叠加顺序为元素添加的先后顺序。覆盖物初始化时如果未设置zIndex参数，默认值为0。异常值按默认值处理。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.169999999999998%">          <p>标记的旋转角度。</p>          <p>以正北方向为0度、顺时针方向为正的角度，默认值为0，取值范围：[0, 360)。超出取值范围的值会换算成取值范围内的值，比如361会被换算成1，-1换算为359。</p> href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource" target="_blank">Resource</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.98%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.8500000000000005%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.169999999999998%">          <p>图标，不传时显示默认图标。</p>          <ul>           <li>图片格式支持jpg、jpeg、png、gif、webp、svg。</li>           <li>string类型入参支持两种格式：            <ul>             <li>资源相对路径格式：图标存放在resources/rawfile，icon参数传入rawfile文件夹下的相对路径。</li>             <li>toDataURL格式（如data:image/png;base64,&lt;图片的Base64字节编码值&gt;）。</li>            </ul></li>          </ul>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>从5.0.0(12)版本开始，icon属性支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource" target="_blank">Resource</a>类型。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>alpha</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.98%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.8500000000000005%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.169999999999998%">          <p>透明度，取值范围[0, 1]，0代表完全透明，1表示完全不透明，默认值为1，异常值按默认值处理。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>anchorU</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.98%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.8500000000000005%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.169999999999998%">          <p>锚点的水平坐标，以图像宽度的比例，建议取值[0, 1]，默认值为0.5，异常值按默认值处理。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>anchorV</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder"       <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.169999999999998%">          <p>锚点的垂直坐标，以图像高度的比例，建议取值[0, 1]，默认值为1，异常值按默认值处理。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.169999999999998%">          <p>是否可以通过长按来拖拽，默认值为false，异常值按默认值处理。</p>          <ul>           <li>true：可拖拽</li> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">MapCircleOptions<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section5282124803117" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>描述MapCircle属性，继承<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section7400647135116">BaseOverlayOptions</a>。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">        <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.830000000000002%">          <p>折线的渐变属性，默认值为false，异常值按默认值处理。</p>          <ul>           <li>true：可渐变</li>           <li>false：不可渐变</li>          </ul>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>customTexture</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr" target="_blank">ResourceStr</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.8500000000000005%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.32%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.830000000000002%">          <p>折线纹理。建议纹理使用没有背景色（透明色）的图片。</p>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>isTextureMappingUsed</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.8500000000000005%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.32%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.830000000000002%">          <p>是否使用贴图的方式处理纹理，默认值为false。</p>          <ul>           <li>true：使用贴图的方式处理纹理</li>           <li>false：不使用贴图的方式处理纹理</li>          </ul>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.3(15)</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>customTextures</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Array&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr" target="_blank">ResourceStr</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a>&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.8500000000000005%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.32%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.830000000000002%">          <p>多个纹理图片。</p>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.3(15)</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>如果同时传入customTexture和customTextures，则呈现customTexture的效果。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>customTextureIndexes</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Array&lt;number&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.8500000000000005%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="6.32%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.830000000000002%">          <p>每个坐标对应的纹理索引。</p>          <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.3(15)</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.3(15)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>如果传入customTextures，则必须传入customTextureIndexes，同时customTextureIndexes的数组长度必须和points数组长度一致，customTextureIndexes每个元素取值必须在0到customTextures数组长度-1的范围内，如果不满足，返回错误码401。</p>           </div></div></div></td> 1078px;">     <h2 id="section20126194774515" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">BasePriorityOverlayParams<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section20126194774515" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>描述气泡、点注释等覆盖物的基础信息，继承<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section7400647135116">BaseOverlayOptions</a>。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder"      <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.25%">          <p>POI的锚点在水平方向上的位置，值的范围为[0, 1]，默认值为0.5，异常值按默认值处理。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>anchorV</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.630000000000001%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">PointAnnotationParams<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th       <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.380000000000003%">          <p>点注释名称与地图POI名称相同时，是否支持去重，默认值为false，异常值按默认值处理。</p>          <ul>           <li>true：支持去重</li>           <li>false：不支持去重</li>          </ul>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content"> href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section230211714264">CollisionRule</a>.ALL，需要同时设置覆盖物碰撞优先级priority属性。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td       <li>图片格式支持jpg、jpeg、png、gif、webp、svg。</li>           <li>string类型入参支持两种格式：            <p>1. 资源相对路径格式：图标存放在resources/rawfile，icon参数传入rawfile文件夹下的相对路径。</p>            <p>2. toDataURL格式（如data:image/png;base64,&lt;图片的Base64字节编码值&gt;）。</p></li>          </ul>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource" target="_blank">Resource</a>类型。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>showIcon</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">BubbleParams<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section10348735114315" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>描述气泡属性，继承<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section20126194774515">BasePriorityOverlayParams</a>。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.6.1.1" width="30%">          <p><strong>名称</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.6.1.2" width="24.97%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.6.1.3" width="7.51%">          <p>只读</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.6.1.4" width="7.2700000000000005%">          <p>可选</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.6.1.5" width="30.25%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>positions</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="24.97%">          <p>Array&lt;Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section20691173773810">LatLng</a>&gt;&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.51%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.2700000000000005%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.25%">          <p>气泡位置，系统基于多个位置段计算图标的适当位置，异常值不处理。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>icons</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="24.97%">          <p>Array&lt;string | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource" target="_blank">Resource</a>&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.51%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.2700000000000005%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30.25%">          <p>气泡图标，异常值不处理。</p>          <ul>           <li>必须提供4个方向的图标，传入的图标宽高需要相同。</li>           <li>图片格式支持jpg、jpeg、png、gif、webp、svg。</li>           <li>string类型入参支持两种格式：            <ul>             <li>资源相对路径格式：图标存放在resources/rawfile，icon参数传入rawfile文件夹下的相对路径。</li>             <li>toDataURL格式（如data:image/png;base64,&lt;图片的Base64字节编码值&gt;）。</li>            </ul></li>          </ul>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>从5.0.0(12)版本开始，icon属性支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource" target="_blank">Resource</a>类型。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div class="p">      <strong>示例：</strong>      <div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section132819018245" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 890px;">     <h2 id="section88850322916" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">VisibleRegion<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section88850322916" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>VisibleRegion包含四个点，这四个点定义了地图相机的四边形可视区域。因为相机可能会倾斜，所以这个多边形也可以是梯形而不一定是矩形。如果相机正好位于可视区域中心上方，则形状为矩形，但如果相机倾斜，则形状将显示为最短边最接近视点的梯形。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 779px;">     <h2 id="section123881566186" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">MapPoint<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" class="cellrowborder" width="29.53%">          <p>Array&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section9436522104316">ClusterItem</a>&gt;</p></td>         <td    <p>待聚合节点数组。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20.77%">          <p>distance</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.53%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="8.89%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.630000000000001%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.18%">          <p>聚合节点聚合的距离，单位：vp。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p>接口提供以下方法，支持聚合项自定义图标。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.9.1.3.1.1" width="42.13%">      <p>Promise&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a>&gt;</p></td>         <td device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">ImageOverlayParams<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section12537418218" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>覆盖物参数。继承<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section7400647135116">BaseOverlayOptions</a>。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.7.1.6.1.1" width="30%">          <p><strong>名称</strong></p></th>         <th class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.7.1.6.1.5" width="29.99%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>bounds</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section96341159111320">LatLngBounds</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>设置基于矩形区域的覆盖物的位置。position和bounds是可选的，但是两个参数需要必填其中一个参数，当两者都入参时，bounds具有更高的优先级。position入参时，width为必填参数。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>position</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section20691173773810">LatLng</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>设置覆盖物的位置。position和bounds是可选的，但是两个参数需要必填其中一个，当两者都入参时，bounds具有更高的优先级。position入参时，width为必填参数。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>width</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>覆盖物的宽度，单位：米，仅当position有值时有效，width为正整数。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>height</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>覆盖物的高度，单位：米，当position和width都有值时才有效，height为正整数。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>anchorU</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>覆盖物的锚点在水平方向上的位置。取值范围：[0,1]。默认值为0.5。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>当bounds有值时，设置anchorU会改变覆盖物的锚点在水平方向上的位置，不会改变bounds的范围。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>anchorV</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>覆盖物的锚点在垂直方向上的位置。取值范围：[0,1]。默认值为0.5。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>当bounds有值时，设置anchorV会改变覆盖物的锚点在垂直方向上的位置，不会改变bounds的范围。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>bearing</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>覆盖物的旋转角度。</p>          <p>以正北方向为0度、顺时针方向为正的角度，默认值为0，取值范围：[0, 360)。超出取值范围的值会换算成取值范围内的值，比如361会被换算成1，-1换算为359。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>clickable</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>覆盖物是否可单击。</p>          <ul>           <li>true：可点击。</li>           <li>false：不可点击。</li>          </ul>          <p>默认值为false。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>image</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr" target="_blank">ResourceStr</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>覆盖物的图像入参。</p>          <p>图片格式支持jpg、jpeg、png、gif、webp、svg。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr" target="_blank">ResourceStr</a>为Resource和string两种格式，其中string类型入参支持两种格式：</p>            <ul>             <li>资源相对路径格式：图标存放在resources/rawfile，image参数传入rawfile文件夹下的相对路径。</li>             <li>toDataURL格式（如data:image/png;base64,&lt;图片的Base64字节编码值&gt;）。</li>            </ul>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>transparency</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.76%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.249999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.99%">          <p>覆盖物的透明度。</p>          <p>取值范围：[0, 1]。</p>          <p>0表示不透明，1表示全透明。</p>          <p>默认值为0。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" = {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">bounds</span>: { <span class="hljs-attr">southwest</span>: { <span class="hljs-attr">latitude</span>: <span class="hljs-number">32</span>, <span  </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 5123px;">     <h2 id="section316117228284" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">BuildingOverlayParams<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section316117228284" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>3D建筑参数。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.7.1.6.1.3" width="10%">          <p>只读</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>points</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>Array&lt;<a <p>限制最大高度30000米。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>floorBottomHeight</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"> <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1448px;">     <h2 id="section16452081559" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">BuildingTexture<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section16452081559" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>建筑纹理。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.7.1.6.1.1" width="30%">          <p><strong>名称</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.7.1.6.1.2" width="25%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.7.1.6.1.3" width="10%">          <p>只读</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.7.1.6.1.4" width="10%">          <p>可选</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.7.1.6.1.5" width="25%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>image</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr" target="_blank">ResourceStr</a> | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-image-pixelmap" target="_blank">image.PixelMap</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>纹理图片。</p>          <p>图片格式支持jpg、jpeg、png、gif、webp、svg。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr" target="_blank">ResourceStr</a>为Resource和string两种格式，其中string类型入参支持两种格式：</p>            <ul>             <li>资源相对路径格式：图标存放在resources/rawfile，image参数传入rawfile文件夹下的相对路径。</li>             <li>toDataURL格式（如data:image/png;base64,&lt;图片的Base64字节编码值&gt;）。</li>            </ul>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>width</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>纹理宽度，单位：米，取值大于等于0，默认值为3，异常值按默认值处理。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>height</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>纹理高度，单位：米，取值大于等于0，默认值为3，异常值按默认值处理。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-xri-c106="" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 4607px;">     <h2 id="section202444375510" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">TraceOverlayParams<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>动态轨迹的参数。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.65%">          <p>points</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.470000000000001%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.66%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.87%">          <p>跟踪点。</p>          <p>points个数上限为100000。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.65%">          <p>width</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="26.35%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.470000000000001%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.66%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="29.87%">          <p>轨迹宽度，单位：px。</p>          <p>默认值为10。</p>          <p>取值范围：[0, 512]，大于512按512处理。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.65%">          <p>color</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="26.35%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.470000000000001%"> <p>默认值为0xaaff0000。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.65%">          <p>isMapMoving</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="26.35%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.470000000000001%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.66%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td  </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.65%">          <p>animationDuration</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="26.35%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td    <p>轨迹动画持续时间，单位为毫秒，最小值为100。</p>          <p>默认值为5000。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>当持续时间小于100毫秒时，时间将按默认值5000毫秒处理。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.65%">          <p>animationCallback</p></td>         <td
